 

THE CONSTITUTION OF INDIA - TELUGU VERSION

[As modified upto the Constitution (104" Amendment) Act, 2019 and
Upto 25™ September, 2020]

NOTE: The first edition of the Telugu version of the Constitution of India was
published on behalf of the Government of India by the active cooperation of the
then Law Department, Government of Andhra Pradesh in the year 1980
incorporating therein amendments to the Constitution upto the Constitution  (44™
Amendment) Act, 1978 with the approval of Ministry of Law and Justice,
Legislative Department, New Delhi.

In this connection, it may be mentioned that incorporating further
amendments during the past 40 years the present translation of telugu version of the
Constitution of India has been prepared by the Law Department, Government of
Telangana and the same has been scrutinized and updated in pursuance of the
directions of the present Secretary, Government of India, Ministry of Law and
Justice, Legislative Department, Official Languages Wing (Regional Languages
Unit) as a part of implementation of the decision of the Central Government to make
available the Constitution of India and other Central Laws to the general public in
their own regional official languages to enable them for better understanding the
same to fulfill the constitutional mandate. The footnotes below the text indicate the
Constitution Amendment Acts and other notified Orders by which such amendments

have been made or passed.
